## 🧠 Expression Engine 2.0 — FACS-Grounded

Every facial beat in this set is coded with an code mapped to real Facial Action Coding System Action Units (AUs) and Ekman's universal-emotion markers. Two rules from the science drive how we shoot them:

- The eyes lead. Fear and anger live in the upper face (brows + lids) and are read more slowly by viewers — so we hold close-ups on the eyes longer for those. Happiness and surprise read almost instantly and can flash.
- Genuine vs. performed. A real smile is Duchenne (cheek-raise + lip-corner pull → crow's-feet, eyes engaged); a fake/social smile is lips-only. Rage is amplified by reddening of the face; effort by the jaw-clench grimace.

| Code | Emotion | Action Units (FACS) | Visible markers |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | Cold focus / game face | faint AU7 + AU23 | near-neutral, level gaze, lids slightly tightened, lips lightly pressed, living stillness |
| | Determination | AU4 + AU7 + AU23/24 + jaw-set | brows knit, lids tight, lips pressed, masseter clenched, steady unblinking aim |
| | Exertion / strike-face | AU4 + jaw-clench + AU9/10 + platysma | the "power face": frown, bared/gritted teeth, nose-wrinkle, neck tendons corded |
| | Anger / fury | AU4 + AU5 + AU7 + AU23 (snarl) | brows down-and-together, hard upper-lid glare, lids tight, lips tight or snarling, face reddening |
| | Fear | AU1+2+4 + AU5 + AU7 + AU20 + AU26 | brows up and drawn (wavy forehead), whites above iris, lids tense, lips stretched, jaw parted |
| | Shock / panic (fear+surprise) | AU1+2+5 (max) + AU26 + head recoil | flash of full sclera, brows shot up, jaw drops, sharp head-snap back |
| | Surprise | AU1+2+5B+26 | brows up-and-curved, lids raised, quick jaw-drop — fastest-read, can flash <0.5s |
| | Awe / wonder | AU1+2 + AU5 + AU26 (relaxed) | brows up, eyes wide without fear-tension, lips parting, gaze soft and lifted |
| | Pain / impact | AU4+6+7+9+10 + AU25/26 | eyes squeezed, nose wrinkled, upper lip raised, grimace, sharp breath |
| | Adrenaline grin (genuine) | AU6 + AU12 (Duchenne) + AU5 | crow's-feet, cheeks up, bright wide eyes, reckless open grin |
| | Triumph / relief | AU6+12 (Duchenne) + slight AU1 + long exhale | eyes-engaged smile, brow easing, shoulders dropping, chest settling |
| | Smug / disdain | R12A + R14A (unilateral) | one-sided lip-corner pull/tighten, cool eyes |
| | Exhaustion | drooped AU43 lids + slack jaw + platysma | heavy lids, parted slack mouth, heaving chest, sweat-sheen, micro-tremor |

Timing law: micro-expressions flash in under 0.5s (use for involuntary "leaks" — a flash of fear under a brave face); macro-expressions hold 0.5–4s (use for the emotional landing of a beat). Every frame below names the code(s) and the transition across the beat.

## 🥊 Combat-Expression Micro-Beat Library

Applied to the punch/kick/impact moments so the face sells the choreography:

- Wind-up: → — the gaze locks and the jaw sets a beat before the limb moves (intent telegraphed in the eyes first).
- Commit / strike: the power-face blooms at peak exertion: jaw-clench, bared teeth, nostril-flare, neck tendons; a sharp kiai-breath.
- Contact (theirs): held + impact-shudder through the cheeks; on the receiver, (eyes squeezed, grimace) landing on guard/gear only.
- Recoil / near-miss: micro-flash (sclera flash + head-snap) resolving back to within the same beat.
- Magic ignition: → — strain releases into wonder as the impossible blooms.
- Resolution: → → — wonder to reckless grin to genuine Duchenne triumph.

## 🎥 Slow-Motion & Close-Up Shot Grammar

- Macro close-up (CU/ECU): at least one frame per concept fills the frame with Aira's eyes/face at the emotional peak — pores, lashes, catchlights, a single bead of sweat or seawater — to land the beat. Held a touch longer for fear/anger (slower-read).
- Slow-motion (ramp): at least one beat per concept ramps to ~120–240fps feel (described as slow-motion) on the signature strike or magic ignition — debris, droplets, petals, sparks suspended; the face crisp inside the slow chaos. We ramp (speed-ramp in/out) rather than running the whole reel slow.
- One camera move per frame still holds (push-in, orbit, track, crane, whip-settle) — slow-mo is a time treatment, not a second move.
- Contact clarity: one strike / one contact per beat, clean silhouette separation, controlled motion-blur on limbs but the face kept crisp and singular.

## 🔒 Locked Invariants (recap)

- Aira from the locked reference sheet only; adult, 25; warm amber-brown eyes; full-coverage, non-sexualized; no physical or ethnic enumeration.
- One impossible magical move + a perfect-loop close per concept.
- Two audio layers: Block A (in-frame diegetic, inside each VIDEO PROMPT) and Block B (a separate 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief outside the prompts, with role, genre, tempo/key, instrumentation-by-layer, dynamic arc, hits, mix, loop-point).
- Codes carried over: real pores/micro-detail · living stillness · push-in.
- Every IMAGE PROMPT carries: Identity Lock, Wardrobe, Footwear, Eye Colour, Accessories, Hair, Makeup, Hands & Nails, Expression, Body Posture & Weight, Spatial Logic, Lighting, Framing, Lens/DOF/Bokeh, Atmosphere, Color Grade, Texture & Micro-Detail, Negative.
- Every VIDEO PROMPT carries: Shot Type, Camera Movement (one), Lens, Physics, Subject + Object Action (timecoded), Expression Transition, Slow-Motion (if any), Lighting, Environment, Audio (Block A), Duration, Frame-rate/Motion-blur, Lip-sync, Negative.

## Concept 1 — Leviathan of the Endless Sea

Lane: Open-ocean survival & evasion (no fight) · one woman, one small boat, and a sky-touching sea monster — the headline spectacle of the set.

Format: Eight-frame vertical reel — one continuous survival encounter in the middle of a vast storm-ocean as a colossal leviathan rises, rendered as eight seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-four seconds, built for maximum emotional reading with a macro close-up and a slow-motion wave-parting beat.

Hero Element: No weapon, no fight — Aira survives and evades through seamanship, nerve, and one impossible act of water-magic. The drama is carried by her face against an overwhelming force.

Antagonist Element: A massive, hyper-realistically rendered sea monster — a leviathan whose head and coils rise sky-high out of the ocean. Treated like a nature-documentary apex animal, not a cartoon: real water-sheeting and displacement, barnacled and scarred hide, slick membranous fins, a vast intelligent eye, immense believable weight and scale, faint deep-sea bioluminescence along its flanks. It is awe-inspiring and dangerous but not gory — the threat is scale, water, and force, never blood.

Setting: The middle of a vast open ocean at storm-dusk — mountainous slate-and-teal swells, a bruised violet-and-gold sky with broken storm-light, sheeting spray and rain, Aira's small weatherbeaten longboat the only human thing for miles.

Wardrobe: A fitted teal-and-charcoal weatherproof sailing jacket with sealed seams, a storm-hood, an integrated climbing-style harness, waterproof trousers over grip sea-boots — full-coverage, modest, mariner-coded, drenched and storm-lashed.

Footwear: Charcoal grip-soled sea-boots, rigid and lugged, braced on the pitching wet deck.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (consistent locked identity), blazing against the storm, catching the leviathan's bioluminescence.

Accessories: A luminous blue-green tide-pendant at her throat (the source of her water-magic, glowing brighter as she calls the sea), fingerless sailing gloves, a rope-harness tether, the thin titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, soaked and rain-slick, tail whipping in the gale.

Makeup: Matte storm-wet complexion, defined brow, cool eye, neutral lip; sea-spray beads and cold-flush permitted.

Movement (the one impossible move): At the climax, as a mountainous wave and the leviathan's bulk bear down together, Aira raises both hands and her tide-pendant flares — and she parts the towering wave into a vast canyon of standing water, two sheer walls of suspended ocean opening a corridor she rides through, the leviathan gliding past its glassy walls.

Concept Line: "Alone on the endless sea, she looked the leviathan in the eye — and split the ocean to live."

Duration: ~24 seconds · 8 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 5).

Mood: Awe, terror, nerve, transcendence — the sublime.

Composition: Towering vertical swells and a sky-filling monster against one small human; macro close-up at the emotional peak; slow-motion at the wave-parting; scale contrast pushed in every frame — tiny boat, vast beast.

Grade: Slate-and-teal ocean, bruised violet-and-gold storm sky, deep-sea bioluminescent cyan on the leviathan, glassy aquamarine for the parted-water magic, rich blacks, controlled bloom on storm-light and spray.

Identity Safety: Aira rendered entirely from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; no physical or ethnic enumeration; full-coverage wardrobe; the monster is awe-and-scale dramatic, never gory; no harm shown to the animal or to her.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score and sound-design bed under the in-frame diegetic audio across all eight frames, binding them into one twenty-four-second piece. Genre & palette: Vast oceanic epic-orchestral — a deep sub-and-cello swell, thunderous taiko and timpani, a low brass leviathan-motif (a slow rising three-note horn-call for the monster), a tense string ostinato, a vast wordless choir reserved for the wave-parting magic, and storm-and-ocean ambience. Tempo & key: 60 BPM half-time feel rising to 120 BPM, C minor resolving to C major at the finale, 4/4, so the swells and the great beats land like breaths of the sea. Instrumentation by layer: sub-and-cello swell (the ocean's mass), taiko and timpani (the monster's movement and the wave-hits), low brass leviathan-motif (the creature's presence), string ostinato (survival tension), vast choir and shimmering glass-harmonica (the water-magic), granular storm-and-spray texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 vast and lonely (sub-swell, wind, and a far cello only); Frame 2 the low-brass leviathan-motif rises with the breach; Frame 3 strings constrict to a held high tremolo over the close-up; Frame 4 taiko and timpani pound under the bearing-down wave; Frame 5 a huge riser collapses into a suspended near-silence and a single sustained choir-note as she parts the wave (the slow-motion peak); Frame 6 the choir and strings soar as she rides the water-canyon; Frame 7 an impact-boom and breath-held silence at the eye-to-eye near-miss; Frame 8 a vast resolving major-key choir-and-brass swell as the sea calms, tailing to the opening sub-swell for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: a deep breach-boom and rising horn on the monster's surfacing (F2), a tremolo-constrict into the close-up (F3), pounding taiko under the wave (F4), a riser-into-silence with one choir-note on the parting (F5), a soaring choir swell through the canyon ride (F6), an impact-boom then near-silence at the near-miss (F7), a triumphant major resolve on the calm (F8). Mix: score about 5 dB under the storm, ocean, and monster sounds at peak; sidechain the bed to the great booms; ultra-wide choir and strings, mono-tight sub; tape warmth, vast cathedral-reverb on the choir, convolution sea-space on the monster calls. Loop point: the closing sub-swell matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 80-second custom cinematic score (8 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on deep trailer percussion, a driving synth bass and brass swells — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a low brass-and-sub impact (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — At the climax, as a mountainous wave and the leviathan's bulk bear down together, Aira raises…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, taut percussive tension as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

### Frame 1 of 8 — IMAGE PROMPT

IDENTITY LOCK: Aira [paste identity-lock reference sheet here]. Scene: she stands braced at the helm of her small longboat in the middle of a vast storm-ocean at dusk, one gloved hand on the tiller, scanning the mountainous swells, utterly alone between sky and sea. WARDROBE: teal-and-charcoal weatherproof sailing jacket, sealed seams, storm-hood blown back, harness snug, drenched. FOOTWEAR: grip sea-boots braced wide on the pitching wet deck. EYE COLOUR: warm amber-brown, storm-light catchlight, scanning the swells. ACCESSORIES: tide-pendant glowing faint blue-green at her throat, sailing gloves, rope-harness tether, titanium cuff. HAIR: tight low braid, soaked, tail whipping in the gale. MAKEUP: matte storm-wet skin, defined brow, cool eye, neutral lip. HANDS & NAILS: short clean nails, one gloved hand gripping the tiller, knuckles set. EXPRESSION: cold-focus game face — faint lid-tighten and lightly pressed lips, level scanning gaze, a slow controlled breath, calm nerve under vast threat, living stillness (breath, rain, sea-heave alive). BODY POSTURE & WEIGHT: braced wide against the pitch, weight low and centered over the deck, shoulders square to the swells. SPATIAL LOGIC: foreground the wet tiller and her braced hand; midground Aira at the helm of the small boat; background mountainous slate-teal swells, a bruised violet-and-gold storm sky, sheeting rain, empty horizon. LIGHTING: KEY broken gold storm-light low from camera-left; FILL cool teal sea-bounce; RIM rain-lit edge on hood and braid; PRACTICAL the faint pendant-glow. FRAMING: ASPECT 9:16, wide, low camera on the deck, the boat tiny against towering swells and sky. SUBJECT FRAMING & POSITION: Framed wide, low camera on the deck, the boat tiny against towering swells and sky, the figure set clearly within the scene. Her body reads braced wide against the pitch, weight low and centered over the deck, shoulders square to the swells. The camera holds the framing's distance, the action sharp and Aira the central figure. The beat: she stands braced at the helm of her small longboat in the middle of a vast storm-ocean at dusk, one gloved hand on the tiller, scanning the mountainous swells. ORIENTATION LOCK — preserve this exact left-to-right composition; do not mirror, flip or invert the frame. LENS + DOF + BOKEH: 28mm-equivalent, f/4, deep focus, sharp on her, spray flecking the lens-feel. ATMOSPHERE: sheeting rain, sea-spray, storm-haze, scale and solitude. COLOR GRADE: slate-and-teal ocean, violet-and-gold sky, deep blacks, controlled storm-light bloom. TEXTURE & MICRO-DETAIL: pores, rain-beads and cold-flush on the skin, sealed-seam jacket weave, wet deck-grain and rope detail, foam-laced swell-faces. NEGATIVE: no other boats or people, no monster yet, no facial blur, no distorted hands, no logos or text, no warped water, no oversaturation, no sexualization, no physical or ethnic enumeration, no watermark.

### Frame 1 of 8 — VIDEO PROMPT

SHOT TYPE: Wide lonely establishing shot, low on the deck. CAMERA MOVEMENT: one move only — a slow 1.2x push-in toward Aira at the helm. LENS: 28mm-equivalent, f/4. PHYSICS: the boat pitches and rolls on mountainous swells; rain sheets; spray bursts off the bow; her braid and hood whip; the pendant glows faintly; no monster yet. SUBJECT + OBJECT ACTION (timecoded): 0.0–1.0s Aira rides the pitch at the tiller, scanning the swells (boat heaving, rain sheeting); 1.0–2.0s a larger swell lifts the bow and she leans into it, gaze sweeping the horizon; 2.0–3.0s the boat settles into a trough, the only motion sea-heave, rain, and whipping braid. EXPRESSION TRANSITION: throughout — level nerve, a faint eye-narrow by 2.5s as something unseen draws her attention; no smile. SLOW-MOTION: none (real-time). LIGHTING: broken gold storm-key, teal sea-fill, faint pendant practical. ENVIRONMENT: vast empty storm-ocean, tiny boat. AUDIO (Block A, in-frame diegetic): a vast wind-and-ocean bed, rain on the hood, hull-creak and rigging-clatter, a bow-spray burst at 1.2s; score sub-swell, wind, and a far cello only. DURATION: 3.0s. FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, 180°, natural blur on rain and sea. LIP-SYNC: none, lips set. NEGATIVE: no cuts, no second camera move, no monster yet, no extra people, no warping, no text.

### Frame 2 of 8 — VIDEO PROMPT

SHOT TYPE: Extreme low up-angle reveal shot — scale-contrast hero beat. CAMERA MOVEMENT: one move only — a slow crane-up following the monster's rise. LENS: 24mm-equivalent, f/5.6. PHYSICS: the leviathan breaches with immense believable weight, ocean sheeting off it in real cascades and a displacement-wave rolling outward to rock the boat hard; spray atomizes; the bioluminescence pulses. SUBJECT + OBJECT ACTION (timecoded): 0.0–0.8s the sea ahead heaves and domes as the leviathan's head and coils surge up, water cascading off (the boat lurching on the displacement); 0.8–2.0s the monster towers to full sky-touching height as Aira's head snaps up and she braces at the gunwale, craning back; 2.0–3.0s the creature holds, vast and dripping, its great eye settling toward the tiny boat. EXPRESSION TRANSITION: nerve breaks into wide-sclera awe at 0.8s, tipping into a gasping fear-flash by 1.6s as the full scale lands. SLOW-MOTION: none (real-time, to sell true weight). LIGHTING: storm-backlight on the monster, cyan bioluminescent fill on her face. ENVIRONMENT: the leviathan towering over the dwarfed boat. AUDIO (Block A): a colossal breach-boom and water-cascade roar, a displacement-gust, a creaking hull-lurch, Aira's sharp caught gasp at 1.0s; score the low-brass leviathan-motif rising under a deep boom. DURATION: 3.0s. FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, 180°, heavy natural blur on cascading water, crisp on her face. LIP-SYNC: none; a gasp. NEGATIVE: no gore, no cartoon look, no warped anatomy, no cut, no second creature, no text.

### Frame 3 of 8 — IMAGE PROMPT (MACRO CLOSE-UP)

IDENTITY LOCK: Aira [paste identity-lock reference sheet here]. Scene: a macro close-up — the frame fills with Aira's face as she stares up at the leviathan, terror and resolve warring in her eyes, seawater streaming down her skin, the monster's cyan glow and the storm reflected in her irises. WARDROBE: only the jacket-collar and hood-edge in frame, drenched. FOOTWEAR: out of frame. EYE COLOUR: warm amber-brown filling the frame, pupils wide, the towering monster and storm mirrored in the wet iris — the emotional anchor of the concept. ACCESSORIES: the pendant-glow underlighting her jaw from below frame, a glint of the cuff. HAIR: soaked braid-strands plastered to the temple and cheek. MAKEUP: matte storm-wet skin, defined brow, cool eye; sea-water sheeting. HANDS & NAILS: one gloved knuckle just entering frame at the jaw, gripping the collar. EXPRESSION (resolving to): fear under command — brows up-and-drawn with a wavy-forehead trace, upper lids raised showing white above the iris, lower lids tense, lips parted and stretched on a shaking breath — then, held a beat longer (fear reads slow), the jaw sets and the lips press as determination takes the fear's place. BODY POSTURE & WEIGHT: implied craned-up tension in the neck tendons (platysma) and a single hard swallow. SPATIAL LOGIC: foreground her face filling the frame; the monster and storm exist only as reflections in her eyes and a soft cyan glow at the frame-edges. LIGHTING: KEY cool cyan bioluminescent up-and-side light from the pendant and monster-glow; FILL faint gold storm-light; RIM rain-light on the cheekbone; catchlights carrying the monster's silhouette. FRAMING: ASPECT 9:16, extreme close-up, eyes on the upper third, a sliver of trembling lip below. SUBJECT FRAMING & POSITION: Framed extreme close-up, eyes on the upper third, a sliver of trembling lip below, the figure set clearly within the scene. Her body reads implied craned-up tension in the neck tendons (platysma) and a single hard swallow. The camera holds the framing's distance, the action sharp and Aira the central figure. The beat: a macro close-up — the frame fills with Aira's face as she stares up at the leviathan, terror and resolve warring in her eyes, seawater streaming down her skin. ORIENTATION LOCK — preserve this exact left-to-right composition; do not mirror, flip or invert the frame. LENS + DOF + BOKEH: 90mm-equivalent macro, f/2.8, razor focus on the iris and lashes, everything else melting to glow-bokeh. ATMOSPHERE: seawater streaming over skin, micro-spray drifting, breath-fog in the cold. COLOR GRADE: cyan-and-gold on wet skin, deep shadow, gentle bloom in the catchlights. ## Concept 2 — Cherry-Blossom Courtyard Duel

Lane: Hand-to-hand wuxia duel (no weapons) — the first of the gem-grade fight concepts, where the face sells every strike.

Format: Seven-frame vertical reel — a single moonlit courtyard duel between Aira and a masked rival duelist, rendered as seven seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-one seconds, choreographed around the Combat-Expression Micro-Beat Library with a macro close-up and a slow-motion spin-kick.

Hero Element: A flowing, athletic wuxia exchange — blocks, flowing parries, a leaping 360° spinning hook kick — every impact landing on guard and forearm, never on flesh; respectful, non-gory, a duel of skill.

Antagonist Element: A masked rival duelist in dark robes — an equal, honorable opponent, fully covered, faceless behind a porcelain half-mask, matching her move for move.

Setting: A moonlit temple courtyard in full cherry-blossom bloom — pale stone tiles, a still black reflecting pond, paper lanterns, an arched gate, blossom trees raining pink-white petals through the cool night air.

Wardrobe: A fitted charcoal-and-plum martial-arts jacket with a wrapped sash, tapered combat trousers, forearm wraps — full-coverage, modest, movement-ready.

Footwear: Soft-soled black martial slippers, silent and flexible on the stone.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), catching moonlight and lantern-glow, locking targets a beat before each strike.

Accessories: A jade focus-bead bracelet (the source of the petal-magic, glowing at the climax), forearm wraps, the thin titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, whipping with each spin.

Makeup: Matte complexion, defined brow, cool eye, neutral lip; effort-sheen permitted.

Movement (the one impossible move): At the kick's apex the falling petals freeze in midair and spiral into a slow-turning vortex around both duelists, suspended like a galaxy of blossom, before drifting free again.

Concept Line: "Two masters, one courtyard of falling blossom — and a heartbeat where even the petals held still."

Duration: ~21 seconds · 7 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 4).

Mood: Grace, tension, mutual respect, transcendence.

Composition: Symmetry across the courtyard, falling-petal depth layers, a macro close-up at the target-lock, slow-motion at the spin-kick and petal-freeze.

Grade: Moonlit blue-silver, warm lantern-amber accents, pink-white blossom, jade-green magic-glow, deep ink-blacks.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage; the duel is skill-based and non-gory; the opponent is fully covered and unharmed.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all seven frames. Genre & palette: Wuxia cinematic — a lone guqin and erhu melody, bamboo dizi flute, soft taiko and frame-drum, plucked pipa for the strikes, a wordless female vocal and shimmering bell-tree reserved for the petal-freeze magic, and night-garden ambience. Tempo & key: 70 BPM rising to 132 BPM at the spin-kick, D minor with a pentatonic color resolving to D major, 4/4, the exchanges landing on the drum-hits. Instrumentation by layer: guqin/erhu (the duel's breath and melody), dizi flute (grace and air), taiko/frame-drum and pipa (the strikes and footwork), wordless vocal and bell-tree/glass-harmonica (the petal-magic), granular night-garden texture (crickets, pond, leaf-rustle). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 sparse guqin and night ambience as they square off; Frame 2 pipa and frame-drum kick in with the first exchange; Frame 3 a held erhu note over the close-up target-lock; Frame 4 a hard taiko-and-pipa burst that drops into suspended hush for the slow-motion kick; Frame 5 the wordless vocal and bell-tree bloom as the petals freeze; Frame 6 the full ensemble flows through the counter; Frame 7 a warm resolving D-major guqin-and-vocal phrase as they bow, tailing to the opening guqin for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: drum-hits on each blocked strike (F2), an erhu-held breath into the close-up (F3), a pipa-burst into slow-motion hush on the kick (F4), a vocal-and-bell bloom on the petal-freeze (F5), an ensemble swell through the counter (F6), a major-key resolve on the bow (F7). Mix: score about 4 dB under the strike and cloth-and-footwork sounds at peak; sidechain to the drum-hits; wide strings and vocal, tight drums; tape warmth, garden-reverb, a long shimmer-tail on the magic. Loop point: the closing guqin matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 70-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — At the kick's apex the falling petals freeze in midair and spiral into a slow-turning vortex…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

NEGATIVE: no gore, no weapons, no face-contact, no cut, no doubled limbs, no face-smear, no text.

## Concept 3 — Sky-Island Cloud Temple Chase

Lane: Free-running leap-chase across floating islands (action, not a straight fight) — built on a varied movement-and-attack vocabulary so no two beats feel the same.

Format: Eight-frame vertical reel — a single continuous rooftop-style chase across a chain of floating sky-temples, rendered as eight seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-four seconds, mixing parkour, one mid-chase clash with multiple attacking methods, a macro close-up, and a slow-motion void-leap.

Hero Element: A relentless, inventive chase — sprint, long-jump, wall-run, vault, slide, plus one mid-chase clash that strings elbow-parry → knee → momentum hip-throw — every technique different, the magic carrying her across the impossible gaps.

Antagonist Element: A masked pursuer (fully covered, faceless), chasing her across the islands — an obstacle and a threat, never harmed; the one clash ends with a throw, not a beating.

Setting: A chain of floating sky-temples at golden dawn — tiered pagodas, stone bridges, prayer-flag lines, and railed terraces drifting in a vast sea of clouds, sunlit peaks breaking through far below, deep blue sky above.

Wardrobe: A fitted slate-and-saffron running tunic with a cross-strap harness, tapered trousers, light forearm wraps — full-coverage, modest, built for speed.

Footwear: Grippy split-sole running shoes, fast and silent on stone.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), reading each gap and ledge a beat ahead.

Accessories: A sky-stone ring on her hand (the source of the cloud-stone magic, glowing as steps form), cross-strap harness, titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, streaming in the wind of the run.

Makeup: Matte complexion, defined brow, cool eye, neutral lip; wind-flush and effort-sheen permitted.

Movement (the one impossible move): As she leaps the chasms between islands, glowing cloud-stone steps materialize under each foot — luminous platforms blossoming from mist exactly where she needs them, dissolving the instant she leaves them.

Concept Line: "She ran out of island and kept running — the sky building a staircase one step ahead of her feet."

Duration: ~24 seconds · 8 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 6).

Mood: Exhilaration, momentum, wonder, nerve.

Composition: Vast vertical drops and sky-depth, leading-line bridges and railings, a macro close-up mid-flight, slow-motion at the great void-leap.

Grade: Dawn gold-and-rose, deep sky-blue, cloud-white, luminous cyan cloud-stone glow, clean shadows.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage; the chase is athletic and non-gory; the pursuer is fully covered and unharmed.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all eight frames. Genre & palette: Soaring adventure-orchestral with propulsive percussion — a driving taiko-and-tom ostinato, pulsing strings, a heroic horn theme, ethnic flute (dizi/bansuri) for the sky, a wordless choir and bell-tree for the cloud-stone magic, and high-altitude wind ambience. Tempo & key: 140 BPM driving, A minor lifting to A major at the summit, 4/4, footfalls and leaps landing on the down-beats. Instrumentation by layer: taiko/tom ostinato (the running pulse), pulsing strings (momentum), heroic horns (the leaps), sky-flute (altitude and wonder), choir and bell-tree (the materializing steps), granular wind texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 the percussion-ostinato launches with the sprint; Frame 2 horns lift on the first gap-leap as steps bloom; Frame 3 strings drive the wall-run and vault; Frame 4 a brief airy suspension over the close-up; Frame 5 hard percussion and low brass under the clash; Frame 6 everything drops to a choir-and-wind hush for the slow-motion void-leap, then booms back; Frame 7 a percussive hit on the landing slide; Frame 8 a soaring A-major horn-and-choir summit swell tailing to the opening ostinato for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: horn-lifts on each leap (F2, F6), string-drive through the parkour (F3), percussion-and-brass under the clash with throw-impact hit (F5), a hush-then-boom on the void-leap (F6), a slide-hit (F7), a major-key summit resolve (F8). Mix: score about 4 dB under footfalls, wind, and impacts at peak; sidechain to the leaps and the throw; wide strings and choir, tight percussion; tape warmth, altitude-air reverb, shimmer-tail on the magic. Loop point: the closing ostinato matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 80-second custom cinematic score (8 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a glassy harp, an airy choir pad and soft weightless textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a shimmering harp sweep over a choir-pad bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — As she leaps the chasms between islands, glowing cloud-stone steps materialize under each foot, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, weightless choir shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

### Frame 5 of 8 — VIDEO PROMPT (THE CLASH · MULTIPLE METHODS)

---

## Concept 4 — Bioluminescent Crystal Cavern

Lane: Acrobatic descent & escape (no fight) — a race downward through a collapsing cavern, built on a varied traversal vocabulary so every beat moves differently.

Format: Seven-frame vertical reel — a single continuous descent-escape through a vast glowing crystal cavern as the entrance caves in above, rendered as seven seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-one seconds, mixing a rappel-slide, a ledge-swing, a gap-leap, a chimney down-climb, and a slow-motion plunge, with a macro close-up.

Hero Element: Pure descent athleticism — slide, swing, leap, down-climb, dive — each technique different, the magic blooming light to guide her way down.

Antagonist Element: No human foe — the threat is the collapsing cavern and the depth; tension comes from falling rock, narrowing time, and the long drop, never from violence.

Setting: A vast underground cavern walled in towering bioluminescent crystals — cyan, violet, and rose formations glowing in the dark, a luminous pool far below, mineral mist, distant water-drip echo, the entrance high above caving in.

Wardrobe: A fitted charcoal-and-teal climbing suit with a low-profile harness, knee and elbow guards, light gloves — full-coverage, modest, built for descent.

Footwear: Sticky-rubber approach shoes for edging and friction.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), lit by the crystal-glow, reading each hold and ledge.

Accessories: A resonance-crystal pendant on her chest (the source of the bloom-magic, ringing crystals alight as she passes), low-profile harness, titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, swinging with each move.

Makeup: Matte complexion, defined brow, cool eye, neutral lip; effort-sheen and mineral-dust permitted.

Movement (the one impossible move): Every crystal she touches or passes blooms with light — resonant ripples of cyan-violet luminescence spreading outward from her hands and feet, the cavern lighting her descent like a living instrument, brightest at the final plunge.

Concept Line: "The mountain was closing above her — so she went down, and the crystals lit the way like she was playing them."

Duration: ~21 seconds · 7 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 6).

Mood: Urgency, wonder, control, awe.

Composition: Deep vertical descent-lines, crystal-glow depth layers, a macro close-up at mid-descent, slow-motion at the plunge.

Grade: Cyan-violet-rose bioluminescence against deep cavern-black, warm skin-tones, luminous pool-glow, gentle bloom.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage; the sequence is athletic and non-gory; no other people; no harm shown.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all seven frames. Genre & palette: Crystalline ambient-orchestral with urgent pulse — a shimmering glass-and-crystal-bowl bed, a ticking marimba/celesta ostinato for the descent, low cello-and-sub tension for the collapse, a pulsing string riser, a wordless choir and bell-tree for the crystal-bloom magic, and cavern-drip ambience. Tempo & key: 110 BPM urgent, F-sharp minor resolving to F-sharp major at the pool, 4/4, the moves landing on the marimba pulse. Instrumentation by layer: glass-and-bowl shimmer (the crystal cavern), marimba/celesta ostinato (the descent clock), low cello/sub and rumble (the collapse), pulsing strings (urgency), choir and bell-tree (the bloom magic), granular drip-and-air texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 a low rumble and the marimba-clock start as she perches; Frame 2 strings drive the rappel-slide as the first crystals bloom; Frame 3 a horn-lift on the swing-and-leap; Frame 4 a held bowl-shimmer over the close-up; Frame 5 ticking tension through the chimney; Frame 6 everything drops to a choir-and-bell hush for the slow-motion plunge, then a soft splash-resolve; Frame 7 a warm F-sharp-major shimmer as she surfaces in the glowing pool, tailing to the opening rumble-and-marimba for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: a collapse-rumble (F1), string-drive on the slide (F2), horn-lift on the leap (F3), bowl-shimmer into the close-up (F4), ticking tension (F5), hush-then-splash on the plunge (F6), major-key resolve at the pool (F7). Mix: score about 4 dB under rockfall, water, and crystal-tones at peak; sidechain to the collapse-hits; ultra-wide shimmer and choir, tight sub; tape warmth, vast cavern-reverb, long shimmer-tail on the magic. Loop point: the closing rumble-and-marimba matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 70-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — Every crystal she touches or passes blooms with light, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

## Concept 5 — Flooded Cathedral Rite

Lane: Water-magic summoning dance (no fight) — a reverent, flowing spell-performance built on a varied movement vocabulary so the grace never goes static.

Format: Eight-frame vertical reel — a single continuous water-rite in a half-flooded cathedral at dusk, rendered as eight seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-four seconds, mixing wading steps, sweeping conjuring forms, a spinning gather, an altar-leap, and a great water-lift, with a macro close-up and a slow-motion orb-lift.

Hero Element: A dancer's spell-craft — wade, sweep, spin, leap, cast, lift, walk — each movement different, the water answering her like a partner; no combat, the drama all in grace, control, and wonder.

Antagonist Element: None — the only "force" is the water itself and the weight of the silent, sacred space; tension is in the difficulty and beauty of the rite.

Setting: A vast half-flooded gothic cathedral at dusk — knee-to-waist-deep still water mirroring the vaulted ceiling, broken stained-glass windows throwing shafts of ruby, sapphire, and gold light across the nave, drowned pews and a submerged altar, dust-motes and silence.

Wardrobe: A fitted deep-indigo ceremonial gown over slim waterproof leggings, with a structured bodice and a long water-resistant overskirt that moves like ink in the water — full-coverage, modest, ceremonial.

Footwear: Slim dark water-shoes, sure-footed on the submerged stone.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), lit by stained-glass color and water-caustics.

Accessories: A tear-drop water-sapphire circlet at her brow (the source of the rite-magic, glowing as the water rises), slim ring-bracelets, the thin titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, a few strands floating at the waterline.

Makeup: Matte complexion with a faint luminous sheen, defined brow, cool eye, soft neutral lip; water-beads permitted.

Movement (the one impossible move): At the rite's peak she throws her arms up and the entire nave's water rises into dozens of floating mirror-orbs — perfect suspended spheres of water hanging in the colored light, each mirroring her and the cathedral, before raining gently back down.

Concept Line: "In the drowned cathedral she lifted her hands — and the flood rose into a hundred silver moons."

Duration: ~24 seconds · 8 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 6).

Mood: Reverence, wonder, control, transcendence.

Composition: Cathedral symmetry and colored light-shafts, water-mirror reflections, a macro close-up at mid-rite, slow-motion at the orb-lift.

Grade: Deep dusk-blue with ruby, sapphire, and gold stained-glass shafts, silver water-caustics, water-sapphire glow, rich shadow.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage ceremonial gown; the rite is serene and non-violent; no other people.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all eight frames. Genre & palette: Sacred ethereal — a vast pipe-organ pad, a wordless cathedral choir (SATB), glass-harmonica and crystal-bowls, a lone cello melody, soft harp arpeggios, and water-and-stone ambience. Tempo & key: 56 BPM largo rising to 92 BPM at the orb-lift, E minor resolving to E major, 3/4 sarabande feel so the movement flows like a slow dance. Instrumentation by layer: organ pad (the cathedral's breath), cello melody (Aira's intent), choir and glass-harmonica (the water-magic), harp arpeggios (the rising water), crystal-bowls (the orbs), granular water-drip-and-reverb texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 a lone organ pad and dripping echo as she wades in; Frame 2 the cello melody enters with the first conjure; Frame 3 harp arpeggios swirl with the spinning gather; Frame 4 a held choir-note over the close-up; Frame 5 the organ swells under the altar-leap and forms; Frame 6 everything blooms into full choir-and-glass-harmonica as the orbs lift, with a suspended hush at the peak; Frame 7 crystal-bowls shimmer as she walks among the orbs; Frame 8 a warm E-major organ-and-choir resolution as the water rains back, tailing to the opening organ pad for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: a cello-entry on the first conjure (F2), a harp-swirl on the spin (F3), a choir-held note into the close-up (F4), an organ-swell on the altar-leap (F5), a full bloom with a hush at the orb-lift peak (F6), a crystal shimmer among the orbs (F7), a major-key resolve as the water falls (F8). Mix: score about 3 dB under the water and stone-reverb sounds at peak; sidechain gently to the orb-lift; ultra-wide choir and organ, intimate cello; tape warmth, vast cathedral-reverb, long shimmer-tail on the magic. Loop point: the closing organ pad matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 80-second custom cinematic score (8 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a glassy harp, an airy choir pad and soft weightless textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a shimmering harp sweep over a choir-pad bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — At the rite's peak she throws her arms up and the entire nave's water rises into…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, weightless choir shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

LIGHTING: gold shaft-key, dusk water-fill, dimming circlet. ENVIRONMENT: the flooded cathedral returning to stillness. AUDIO (Block A): a shimmering rain of water and droplet-patter, the slosh of refilling, settling dripping reverb, a long peaceful exhale; score a warm E-major organ-and-choir resolution tailing to the opening organ pad for the loop. DURATION: 3.0s. FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps with the 48fps orb-rain settle, 180°, gentle blur on falling water, crisp face. LIP-SYNC: none; a peaceful exhale and a smile. NEGATIVE: no gore, no weapons, no cut, no second move, no extra people, no warped geometry, no text or watermark.

---

## Concept 6 — Lantern Festival on Black Water

Lane: Agility & balance traversal (no fight) — a light-footed crossing of a lantern-strewn night lake, built on a varied movement vocabulary so each beat moves differently.

Format: Seven-frame vertical reel — a single continuous traversal across boats, ropes, and rafts on a black festival lake, rendered as seven seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-one seconds, mixing a prow-balance, a rope-beam balance-run, boat-to-boat leaps, a punt-pole vault, and a plank-run, with a macro close-up and a slow-motion light-dragon.

Hero Element: Pure balance and agility — balance, run, leap, vault, slide — each technique different, the lanterns answering her crossing; no combat, the drama all in poise, daring, and wonder.

Antagonist Element: None — the only stakes are the black water below and the gaps to clear; tension comes from balance and timing, never from violence.

Setting: A vast black festival lake at night, surfaced with thousands of floating paper lanterns — warm gold and red glows mirrored on still dark water, moored boats and lantern-rafts, a great lantern-laden barge in the distance, temple lights on the far shore, a thin mist.

Wardrobe: A fitted dark-crimson festival tunic with gold embroidery over slim black leggings and a short structured sash, light wrap-guards on the forearms — full-coverage, modest, agile.

Footwear: Split-sole grip slippers for balance on rope and wood.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), lit gold by the lanterns.

Accessories: A small lantern-amber pendant (the source of the light-magic, glowing as the lanterns answer her), the sash-knot, the thin titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, swinging with each leap.

Makeup: Matte complexion warm-lit, defined brow, cool eye, soft neutral lip; effort-sheen permitted.

Movement (the one impossible move): As she crosses, the floating lanterns lift from the water and gather into a coiling dragon of living light that surges and arcs over the lake beside her, before dispersing back into a thousand rising lanterns.

Concept Line: "She ran across the lantern-lake — and ten thousand little flames rose up into a dragon to run beside her."

Duration: ~21 seconds · 7 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 6).

Mood: Festivity, daring, wonder, triumph.

Composition: Lantern-mirrored water and depth, balance-lines and leaps, a macro close-up at mid-crossing, slow-motion at the light-dragon.

Grade: Warm gold-and-red lantern-glow against deep black water, mirrored reflections, amber pendant-glow, soft mist-bloom.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage festival wear; the crossing is athletic and non-violent; no other people on her path.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all seven frames. Genre & palette: Festival cinematic-orchestral with East-Asian color — taiko and festival-drum pulse, erhu and dizi-flute melody, plucked guzheng, temple-bells and wind-chimes, a wordless choir and brass for the light-dragon, and water-and-night ambience. Tempo & key: 100 BPM building to 132 BPM at the dragon, D minor resolving to D major, 4/4 with a driving festival pulse so the leaps land on the drums. Instrumentation by layer: taiko/festival-drums (the crossing's drive), erhu/dizi melody (Aira's line), guzheng plucks (the lanterns), temple-bells and chimes (the festival air), choir and brass (the light-dragon), granular water-and-night texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 a soft guzheng-and-bell bed and distant festival murmur as she balances on the prow; Frame 2 the taiko pulse starts under the rope-run; Frame 3 the erhu lifts as the first lanterns rise on her leap; Frame 4 a held flute-note over the close-up; Frame 5 the drums drive hard under the vault; Frame 6 full choir-and-brass blooms as the light-dragon coils, with a soaring swell; Frame 7 a triumphant D-major hit on the barge-prow, settling to bells as the dragon disperses, tailing to the opening guzheng-and-bell bed for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: a taiko-start on the rope-run (F2), an erhu-lift on the first lantern-rise (F3), a held flute into the close-up (F4), a drum-drive on the vault (F5), a choir-and-brass bloom on the dragon (F6), a triumphant major hit on the barge (F7). Mix: score about 3 dB under the drums, water, and lantern-whoosh at peak; sidechain to the taiko hits; wide choir and bells, tight drums; tape warmth, lake-night reverb, long shimmer-tail on the dragon. Loop point: the closing guzheng-and-bell bed matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 70-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — As she crosses, the floating lanterns lift from the water and gather into a coiling dragon…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

### Frame 6 of 7 — VIDEO PROMPT (THE LIGHT-DRAGON · SLOW-MOTION)

## Concept 7 — Monsoon Rooftop Garden

Lane: Hand-to-hand fight in a thunderstorm — a duel built on a varied attacking vocabulary so no two beats repeat a move; non-gory, impacts landing on guard, gear, and the wet ground.

Format: Eight-frame vertical reel — a single continuous rooftop duel in driving monsoon rain, rendered as eight seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-four seconds, mixing a jab-cross-elbow combo, a knee, a spinning back-elbow, a spinning roundhouse, a leg-sweep, and a hip-throw, with a macro strike close-up and a slow-motion kick.

Hero Element: Storm-fighting choreography — jab, cross, elbow, knee, spin-elbow, roundhouse, sweep, throw — every beat a different technique, expression-driven, ending in mutual respect; non-gory throughout.

Antagonist Element: A skilled masked rival in dark rain-gear who tests her with feints and counters; clean martial contest, never brutal — impacts read on guard, forearms, and the wet rooftop.

Setting: A lush rooftop garden atop a tower at night in a heavy monsoon — potted maples and ferns thrashing in the wind, a shallow flooded stone deck, glass railings streaming water, neon city-glow below, lightning forking across the sky.

Wardrobe: A fitted slate-grey martial top with a water-shedding short jacket, reinforced gloves, slim tactical trousers, a sash-belt — full-coverage, modest, soaked and clinging realistically.

Footwear: Grip martial-arts flats sure on the flooded stone.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), lit by lightning and neon, sharp through the rain.

Accessories: A storm-glass pendant (the source of the rain-magic, flaring as the rain freezes), reinforced gloves, the thin titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, rain-soaked and whipping.

Makeup: Matte complexion sheeted with rain, defined brow, cool eye, neutral lip; rain-and-effort sheen throughout.

Movement (the one impossible move): At each clean strike the falling rain freezes midair into suspended droplets and fine ice-crystal around the impact — the storm holding its breath — then releases and falls again; at the peak a whole field of rain freezes in the air at once.

Concept Line: "They fought in the monsoon — and every time she landed clean, the rain stopped falling and hung in the air like glass."

Duration: ~24 seconds · 8 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 5).

Mood: Tension, power, control, awe, respect.

Composition: Storm-wide and tight strike-angles, rain-freeze accents, a macro close-up early, slow-motion at the spinning kick.

Grade: Cool storm-blue and steel with neon accents, rain-sheen, storm-glass flares of frozen rain, lightning-white pops.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage soaked martial wear; clean non-gory contest; one rival, no blood, no harm shown.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all eight frames. Genre & palette: Percussive hybrid-orchestral storm-combat — taiko and frame-drums, sub-bass thunder, tense staccato strings, a low brass motif, metallic and glassy hits for the rain-freeze, a wordless choir swell at the peak, and rain-and-thunder ambience. Tempo & key: 128 BPM driving, C minor, 4/4 with strikes landing on the down-beats. Instrumentation by layer: taiko/frame-drums (the fight's drive), sub-bass and thunder (the storm), staccato strings (tension and exchanges), low brass (power), glassy crystal-hits and choir (the rain-freeze magic), granular rain-and-wind texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 a low brass-and-thunder bed and tense string-tremolo at the square-off; Frame 2 the taiko drops on the opening combo; Frame 3 a held string-note over the close-up; Frame 4 a heavy hit on the knee and a glassy chime as rain first freezes; Frame 5 everything ramps then drops to a choir-and-glass hush for the slow-motion roundhouse, with a crystalline shimmer; Frame 6 hard drums on the sweep-and-throw; Frame 7 a thunderclap and full choir as the whole rain-field freezes; Frame 8 a resolving C-minor-to-major brass swell as the rain releases and the rivals bow, tailing to the opening bed for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: a taiko-drop on the combo (F2), held string into the close-up (F3), a heavy hit and glass-chime on the knee (F4), a hush-and-shimmer on the slow-mo kick (F5), drum-hits on the sweep-throw (F6), a thunderclap-and-choir on the full freeze (F7), a respectful resolve at the bow (F8). Mix: score about 3 dB under the thunder, rain, and impacts at peak; sidechain hard to the strike-hits; wide thunder and choir, tight drums; tape warmth, rooftop-and-storm reverb, glassy tail on the freeze. Loop point: the closing storm-bed matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 80-second custom cinematic score (8 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on deep trailer percussion, a driving synth bass and brass swells — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a low brass-and-sub impact (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — At each clean strike the falling rain freezes midair into suspended droplets and fine ice-crystal around…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, taut percussive tension as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

## Concept 8 — Desert Moon Oasis

Lane: Movement & dance showcase (no fight) — a flowing solo dance under a vast moon, built on a varied movement vocabulary so every beat moves differently.

Format: Seven-frame vertical reel — a single continuous moonlit dance at a desert oasis, rendered as seven seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-one seconds, mixing gliding steps, a grand jeté, a turn sequence, a floor-rise extension, and a water-run leap, with a macro close-up and a slow-motion moon-path.

Hero Element: Pure dance athleticism and grace — glide, leap, turn, rise, run, balance — each movement different, the moonlight answering her body; no combat, the drama all in line, control, and wonder.

Antagonist Element: None — only the vast silent desert night and the stillness of the moonlit water; tension is in the beauty and difficulty of the dance.

Setting: A desert oasis at night under an enormous low moon — silver dunes rolling to the horizon, a still moonlit pool ringed by date-palms, fine sand glittering, a warm breeze, utter silence but for the wind.

Wardrobe: A fitted silver-grey dance bodice with a long flowing chiffon skirt and slim under-leggings, light wrap-sandals laced at the ankle, a fine sash — full-coverage, modest, built to move like moonlight.

Footwear: Soft lace-up dance sandals, sure on sand and the pool's edge.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), silvered by the moon.

Accessories: A moonstone circlet (the source of the moonlight-magic, glowing as the light gathers), fine wrist-bangles, the thin titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, a few strands lifting in the breeze.

Makeup: Matte complexion with a luminous moon-sheen, defined brow, cool eye, soft neutral lip.

Movement (the one impossible move): As she dances the moonlight gathers into luminous ribbons and a glowing path beneath her feet and around her body — silver light woven by her movement — culminating in a radiant path of moonlight laid across the surface of the pool that she dances along.

Concept Line: "She danced at the oasis and the moonlight followed her feet — until it laid a silver road across the water."

Duration: ~21 seconds · 7 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 6).

Mood: Serenity, grace, wonder, transcendence.

Composition: Vast moon and dune symmetry, moonlit-water reflections, moonlight-ribbon accents, a macro close-up at mid-dance, slow-motion at the moon-path.

Grade: Silver-blue moonlight over warm sand-tones, mirrored pool, moonstone glow, soft bloom.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage flowing dancewear; the dance is serene and non-violent; no other people.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all seven frames. Genre & palette: Ethereal world-fusion — a ney and duduk melody, soft frame-drum and hand-percussion, warm strings, harp arpeggios, a wordless choir and crystal-bells for the moonlight-magic, and desert-night ambience. Tempo & key: 72 BPM building to 104 BPM at the moon-path, A minor resolving to A major, 6/8 lilting so the movement flows like a slow dance. Instrumentation by layer: ney/duduk (Aira's line), frame-drum and hand-percussion (the dance's pulse), warm strings (depth), harp arpeggios (the gathering light), choir and crystal-bells (the moonlight-magic), granular wind-and-sand texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 a lone ney and soft wind as she poses; Frame 2 the frame-drum and harp enter as the first ribbons gather; Frame 3 strings lift on the grand jeté; Frame 4 a held choir-note over the close-up; Frame 5 harp arpeggios swirl through the turns; Frame 6 full choir-and-crystal-bells bloom as the moon-path forms, with a soaring swell; Frame 7 a warm A-major resolution as she settles into the arabesque, tailing to the opening ney for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: a drum-and-harp entry on the first ribbons (F2), a string-lift on the jeté (F3), a held choir into the close-up (F4), a harp-swirl through the turns (F5), a choir-and-bell bloom on the moon-path (F6), a major-key resolve at the arabesque (F7). Mix: score about 3 dB under the wind, water, and shimmer at peak; gentle sidechain to the moon-path bloom; wide choir and strings, intimate ney; tape warmth, vast desert-reverb, long shimmer-tail on the magic. Loop point: the closing ney matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 70-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — As she dances the moonlight gathers into luminous ribbons and a glowing path beneath her feet…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

## Concept 9 — Grand Opera House Escape

Lane: Acrobatic chase & escape (no fight) — a daring traversal across a grand opera house, built on a varied movement vocabulary so every beat moves differently.

Format: Eight-frame vertical reel — a single continuous acrobatic escape through a gilded opera house at night, rendered as eight seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-four seconds, mixing a balcony vault, a curtain-swing, a rigging-cable balance-run, a chandelier-crystal traverse, and a banister-slide, with a macro close-up and a slow-motion crystal-galaxy.

Hero Element: Pure acrobatic escape — vault, swing, balance, leap, traverse, slide, drop — each technique different, the chandelier's crystals turning her path into a galaxy; no combat, the drama all in daring, poise, and wonder.

Antagonist Element: Distant pursuers far below on the orchestra floor — never reached, never fought; the stakes are height, gaps, and getting away clean.

Setting: An opulent gilded opera house at night — tiers of red-velvet box-balconies, gold-leaf scrollwork, a vast painted ceiling, a colossal crystal chandelier glowing dim, work-lights and a single stage-spotlight, deep shadow in the empty house.

Wardrobe: A fitted midnight-blue performance suit with subtle gold piping, a short structured jacket, light gloves, slim trousers, a sash — full-coverage, modest, built for acrobatics.

Footwear: Soft split-sole grip boots for rail, cable, and banister.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), lit gold by the house-lights and chandelier.

Accessories: A crystal-drop pendant (the source of the chandelier-magic, glowing as the crystals answer), light gloves, the thin titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid, swinging with each move.

Makeup: Matte complexion gold-lit, defined brow, cool eye, soft neutral lip; effort-sheen permitted.

Movement (the one impossible move): When she reaches the great chandelier its thousands of crystals detach and hang suspended in the air like a galaxy, becoming luminous stepping-stones she traverses, before drifting back together into a reformed chandelier.

Concept Line: "They chased her up into the gold and the dark — so she ran across a chandelier that came apart into a galaxy of glass."

Duration: ~24 seconds · 8 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 6).

Mood: Daring, elegance, wonder, triumph.

Composition: Vertical opera-house tiers and gold depth, chandelier-crystal accents, a macro close-up early, slow-motion at the crystal-galaxy.

Grade: Warm gold and deep crimson against shadowed black, crystal-sparkle, pendant-glow, single spotlight-white, soft bloom.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage performance suit; the escape is athletic and non-violent; pursuers distant and never engaged.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all eight frames. Genre & palette: Dramatic operatic-orchestral — sweeping strings, brass stabs, a wordless soprano vocalise, harp glissandi, timpani and low percussion, glassy crystal-bells for the chandelier-magic, and empty-house ambience. Tempo & key: 116 BPM driving, G minor resolving to G major, 4/4 with leaps landing on the brass stabs. Instrumentation by layer: driving strings (the chase), brass stabs and timpani (the danger and leaps), soprano vocalise (Aira's daring line), harp glissandi (the movement), glassy crystal-bells and choir (the chandelier-galaxy), granular room-tone-and-creak texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 a tense low-string-and-timpani bed as she perches; Frame 2 strings drive on the vault-and-swing; Frame 3 a held soprano note over the close-up; Frame 4 staccato strings tick under the cable-run; Frame 5 a harp glissando and choir-swell as the crystals detach; Frame 6 full choir-and-crystal-bells bloom for the slow-motion galaxy-traverse, with a soaring vocalise; Frame 7 brass drives the banister-slide and stage-leap; Frame 8 a triumphant G-major brass-and-soprano resolution in the spotlight, tailing to the opening bed for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: a string-drive on the vault-swing (F2), a held soprano into the close-up (F3), staccato tick on the cable-run (F4), a harp-and-choir swell on the crystal-detach (F5), a full bloom on the galaxy-traverse (F6), brass on the banister-slide (F7), a triumphant resolve in the spotlight (F8). Mix: score about 3 dB under the creaks, whooshes, and crystal-tones at peak; sidechain to the brass stabs; wide soprano and strings, tight timpani; tape warmth, grand-hall reverb, glassy tail on the crystals. Loop point: the closing house-bed matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 80-second custom cinematic score (8 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a glassy harp, an airy choir pad and soft weightless textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a shimmering harp sweep over a choir-pad bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — When she reaches the great chandelier its thousands of crystals detach and hang suspended in the…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, weightless choir shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

---

## Concept 10 — Salt-Flat Mirror at Dusk

Lane: Hand-to-hand fight against her own risen reflection — a duel built on a varied attacking vocabulary so no two beats repeat a move; non-gory, the "opponent" a reflection that dissolves to water.

Format: Seven-frame vertical reel — a single continuous mirror-duel on a flooded salt flat at dusk, rendered as seven seeded keyframes, roughly twenty-one seconds, mixing a jab-cross, a palm-strike, a spinning back-fist, a knee, a spinning hook kick, and a sweep-into-throw, with a macro strike close-up and a slow-motion mirrored kick.

Hero Element: Expression-driven mirror-choreography — jab, cross, palm, back-fist, knee, hook-kick, sweep, throw — every beat a different technique, often mirrored then diverging; a duel with the self that ends in self-acceptance; non-gory throughout.

Antagonist Element: Her own reflection risen from the mirror-water as a living double — same face, same skill; not an enemy to destroy but a self to reconcile, dissolving into a splash of water when "defeated."

Setting: A vast salt flat at dusk under a thin sheet of water, making a flawless mirror to the horizon — a burning orange-pink-violet sky doubled perfectly below, distant mountains, hexagonal salt-crust visible at the edges, utter stillness.

Wardrobe: A fitted dust-rose martial top with a wrapped sash, light gloves, slim trousers, forearm guards — full-coverage, modest; the reflection-double wears the identical outfit, mirror-reversed.

Footwear: Grip martial flats sure on the slick mirror-surface.

Eye Colour: Warm amber-brown (locked), lit by the dusk-glow.

Accessories: A mirror-quartz pendant (the source of the reflection-magic, glowing as the double rises and dissolves), forearm guards, the thin titanium wrist cuff.

Hair: The same tight low braid; the double's braid falls over the opposite shoulder.

Makeup: Matte complexion dusk-lit, defined brow, cool eye, neutral lip; effort-sheen throughout.

Movement (the one impossible move): Her reflection rises out of the mirror-water as a living double and fights her move-for-move; at the duel's end the double dissolves back into a splash of mirror-water and melts into the flat, restoring her single reflection.

Concept Line: "At dusk the salt flat became a mirror — and her reflection stood up to fight her, until she made peace with it."

Duration: ~21 seconds · 7 frames · 24fps · 180° shutter (slow-motion ramp on Frame 5).

Mood: Tension, introspection, power, awe, peace.

Composition: Perfect mirror-symmetry and dusk-color, water-spray accents, a macro close-up at mid-duel, slow-motion at the mirrored kick.

Grade: Burning orange-pink-violet dusk doubled on silver water, warm skin, mirror-quartz glow, soft bloom.

Identity Safety: Aira from the locked reference sheet; adult, 25; full-coverage martial wear; clean non-gory contest with a reflection that dissolves to water; no blood, no harm shown.

### 🎚️ Master Soundtrack & Sound-Design Brief — Audio Block B (outside the prompts)

Role: The continuous score under the in-frame diegetic audio across all seven frames. Genre & palette: Introspective hybrid-orchestral with mirrored motifs — a doubled string melody (one part its own delayed reflection), soft taiko and frame-drums, a low cello, glassy water-bells for the mirror-magic, a wordless choir at the reconciliation, and salt-flat wind ambience. Tempo & key: 112 BPM, D minor resolving to D major, 4/4 with strikes on the down-beats and the melody literally echoing itself like a reflection. Instrumentation by layer: doubled/echoed strings (self and reflection), soft taiko (the duel's pulse), low cello (introspection), glassy water-bells and choir (the mirror-magic), granular wind-and-water texture (atmosphere). Dynamic arc: Frame 1 a lone cello and wind, with a single delayed echo entering as the double rises; Frame 2 taiko drops on the first exchange; Frame 3 a held string over the close-up; Frame 4 driving doubled strings through the back-fist exchange; Frame 5 everything drops to a choir-and-water-bell hush for the slow-motion mirrored kick; Frame 6 a swelling, softening choir as the double dissolves to water; Frame 7 a warm D-major resolution as her single reflection is restored, tailing to the opening cello for a perfect loop. Hits & transitions: an echo-entry as the double rises (F1–F2), a taiko-drop on the first exchange (F2), a held string into the close-up (F3), driving doubled strings on the back-fist (F4), a hush on the slow-mo kick (F5), a softening choir on the dissolve (F6), a major-key resolve at the restored mirror (F7). Mix: score about 3 dB under the water-spray and impacts at peak; sidechain to the strike-hits; wide doubled strings and choir, intimate cello; tape warmth, vast flat-reverb, watery tail on the magic. Loop point: the closing cello matches bar one.

MASTER AUDIO: a 70-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 10s) composed in self-resolving ~10-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — Her reflection rises out of the mirror-water as a living double and fights her move-for-move, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

### Frame 1 of 7 — IMAGE PROMPT

IDENTITY LOCK: Aira [paste identity-lock reference sheet here]. Scene: Aira stands alone on the flooded salt flat at dusk, her reflection flawless in the mirror-water beneath her — and the reflection has just begun to rise, its head and shoulders lifting up out of the surface as a living double. WARDROBE: dust-rose martial top, wrapped sash, gloves, slim trousers, forearm guards. FOOTWEAR: grip flats on the slick mirror-surface. EYE COLOUR: warm amber-brown, dusk-lit, widening at the rising double. ACCESSORIES: mirror-quartz pendant (beginning to glow), forearm guards, titanium cuff. HAIR: tight low braid; the rising reflection's braid over the opposite shoulder. MAKEUP: matte dusk-lit, defined brow, cool eye, neutral lip. HANDS & NAILS: short clean nails, gloved hands loose but rising toward a guard. EXPRESSION (into): calm tipping into startled recognition — a level gaze snapping to lifted brows and widened eyes, lips parting, a caught breath as her reflection rises; living stillness. BODY POSTURE & WEIGHT: upright and still, weight settling back as she registers the double, hands lifting. SPATIAL LOGIC: foreground the mirror-water and the rising reflection's head-and-shoulders; midground Aira standing; background the doubled burning dusk-sky and distant mountains. LIGHTING: KEY the burning dusk-glow from the horizon; FILL the mirror-water bounce from below; RIM dusk-edge on braid and shoulders; PRACTICAL the faint pendant. FRAMING: ASPECT 9:16, symmetrical wide with the perfect mirror. SUBJECT FRAMING & POSITION: Framed symmetrical wide with the perfect mirror, the figure set clearly within the scene. Her body reads upright and still, weight settling back as she registers the double, hands lifting. The camera holds the framing's distance, the action sharp and Aira the central figure. The beat: aira stands alone on the flooded salt flat at dusk, her reflection flawless in the mirror-water beneath her — and the reflection has just begun to rise. ORIENTATION LOCK — preserve this exact left-to-right composition; do not mirror, flip or invert the frame. LENS + DOF + BOKEH: 35mm-equivalent, f/2.8, sharp on Aira and the rising reflection, the flat to soft bokeh. ATMOSPHERE: utter stillness, thin water-sheen, dusk-haze. COLOR GRADE: orange-pink-violet dusk doubled on silver water, warm skin, mirror-quartz glow. TEXTURE & MICRO-DETAIL: pores and dusk-sheen, salt-crust at the edges, flawless water-mirror, fabric-weave. NEGATIVE: no gore, no weapons, no blood, no extra people, no facial blur, no distorted hands, no logos or text, no oversaturation, no sexualization, no enumeration, no watermark.

### Frame 1 of 7 — VIDEO PROMPT

SHOT TYPE: Symmetrical wide establishing — the reflection begins to rise. CAMERA MOVEMENT: one move only — a slow push-in toward Aira and her mirror. LENS: 35mm-equivalent, f/2.8. PHYSICS: the water lies mirror-still; the reflection lifts up out of the surface with water sheeting off it as a living double forms; the pendant glows. SUBJECT + OBJECT ACTION (timecoded): 0.0–1.0s Aira stands alone, her reflection flawless below; 1.0–2.0s the reflection begins to rise, head and shoulders lifting out of the water; 2.0–3.0s she startles and lifts her hands toward a guard as the double stands. EXPRESSION TRANSITION: calm tipping into startled recognition by 2.2s. SLOW-MOTION: none (real-time). LIGHTING: dusk-glow key, mirror-water fill, faint pendant practical. ENVIRONMENT: the flooded salt flat at dusk. AUDIO (Block A, in-frame diegetic): vast wind-hush, a soft watery rise, a caught breath; score a lone cello and wind with a single delayed echo entering. DURATION: 3.0s. FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, 180°, gentle blur on rising water. LIP-SYNC: none; a breath. NEGATIVE: no cuts, no second camera move, no weapons, no blood, no warping, no text.
